</style><script type="text/javascript" class="ins-camp-frameless-js ins-camp-frameless-js-665">try {(function(camp){(function (self) {
    self.feedSettings = camp.predictiveFeedSettings;
    self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper = '.ins-preview-wrapper-' + camp.id + ' .ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-main-wrapper';
    self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule = self.feedSettings.feedType === 'systemRule';

    self.getRecommendationFeed = function () {
        if (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule) {
            return spApi.systemRuleRecommendationFeed || self.feedSettings.endpoints;
        }

        return spApi.recommendationFeed || self.feedSettings.endpoints;
    };

    self.getProductFeedEndpoint = function () {
        recFeed = self.getRecommendationFeed();

        if (!recFeed) {
            return false;
        }

        var endpoint = recFeed['serviceUrl'] + recFeed[self.feedSettings.feedSource];

        endpoint = endpoint.replace('{userId}', spApi.storageData('spUID'));
        endpoint = endpoint.replace('{partnerId}', self.feedSettings.pId);
        endpoint = endpoint.replace('{size}', self.feedSettings.feedSize);

        if (spApi.isOnProductPage() &amp;&amp; typeof spApi.getCurrentProduct().id !== 'undefined') {
            if ((!self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; ['similarViewed', 'similarBought'].indexOf(self.feedSettings.feedSource) &gt; -1) ||
                self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule
            ) {
                endpoint = endpoint.replace('{itemId}', spApi.getCurrentProduct().id);
                endpoint = self.createCategoryInfo(endpoint, spApi.getCurrentProduct().cats || []);
            }
        } else if (spApi.isOnCategoryPage() &amp;&amp;
            self.applyFeedTypesCondition(
                [
                    'userBased',
                    'mostPurchased',
                    'mostViewed',
                    'mostViewedOfCat',
                    'mostBoughtOfCat',
                    'mixedStrategy',
                    'highestDiscounted',
                    'trendingProducts',
                    'newArrivals'
                ],
                ['mostViewedOfCat', 'mostBoughtOfCat']
            )
        ) {
            endpoint = self.createCategoryInfo(endpoint, spApi.getCategories());
        } else if (spApi.isOnCartPage() &amp;&amp;
            spApi.getPaidProducts().length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp;
            self.applyFeedTypesCondition(
                ['userBased', 'mostViewed', 'mostPurchased', 'similarViewed', 'similarBought', 'mixedStrategy', 'checkoutRecommendation'],
                ['similarViewed', 'similarBought']
            )
        ) {
            var paidProducts = spApi.getPaidProducts();

            endpoint = self.generateEndpointItemId(endpoint, paidProducts);

            if (!endpoint) {
                sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).hide();
                return '';
            }

            if ((spApi.storageData('prodCats') || []).length &gt; 0) {
                sQuery.each(JSON.parse(spApi.storageData('prodCats')), function (index, value) {
                    if ((paidProducts[0] || {}).id == value.id) {
                        endpoint = self.createCategoryInfo(endpoint, value.cat.split('|'));
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        if (self.feedSettings.feedSource === 'mixedStrategy') {
            var mixedStrategies = '';
            var mixedStrategyUrlMappings = {
                userBased: 'ub',
                mostViewed: 'mvop',
                mostPurchased: 'mpop',
                similarViewed: 'vtv',
                similarBought: 'btb',
                mostViewedOfCat: 'mvoc',
                mostBoughtOfCat: 'mpoc',
                manualMerchandising: 'pd'
            };
            var productIds = [];

            sQuery.each(self.feedSettings.mixedProducts, function (index, item) {
                mixedStrategies += '"' + mixedStrategyUrlMappings[item.strategyName] + '"';
                if (index &lt; self.feedSettings.mixedProducts.length - 1) {
                    mixedStrategies += ',';
                }

                if (item.strategyName === 'manualMerchandising') {
                    productIds.push(item.value);
                }
            });

            if (productIds.length &gt; 0) {
                endpoint = endpoint.replace('{productIds}', productIds.join(','));
            } else {
                endpoint = endpoint.replace('&amp;productIds={productIds}', '');
            }

            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{mixedStrategies}', mixedStrategies);
        }

        if (self.feedSettings.feedSource === 'manualMerchandising') {
            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{productId}', self.feedSettings.manualProducts.join(','));
        }

        if (self.feedSettings.feedSource === 'locationBased') {
            endpoint = self.getLocationBasedEndPoint(endpoint);
        }

        if (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule) {
            var filterUrl = '';

            if ((self.feedSettings.filters || []).length &gt; 0) {
                sQuery.each(self.feedSettings.filters, function (index, filter) {
                    filterUrl += '&amp;filter=' +
                        '[' + filter.attribute.attributeName + ']' +
                        '[' + filter.operator.operator + ']' +
                        '[' + encodeURIComponent(filter.value) + ']';
                });
            }

            if (spApi.isOnProductPage()) {
                filterUrl += '&amp;filter=[item_id][!=][' + spApi.getCurrentProduct().id + ']';
            }

            if (spApi.isOnCartPage()) {
                sQuery.each(spApi.getCartProductStorage(), function (index, product) {
                    filterUrl += '&amp;filter=[item_id][!=][' + product.id + ']';
                });
            }

            endpoint += filterUrl;
            endpoint = endpoint.replace(/{currency}/g, spApi.getCurrency());
            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{language}', spApi.getLocale());
        }

        if (!self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; (self.feedSettings['feedLang'] !== 'tr_TR')) {
            endpoint = endpoint + '&amp;lang=' + self.feedSettings['feedLang'];
        }

        return self.replaceUnUsedUrlParameters(endpoint);
    };

    self.replaceUnUsedUrlParameters = function (endpoint) {
        return endpoint.replace(
            /&amp;productId={itemId}|category={category}&amp;|&amp;category={category}|subCategory={subcategory}&amp;|&amp;subCategory={subCategory}|&amp;country={country}|&amp;city={city}/gi,
            ''
        );
    };

    self.getLocationBasedEndPoint = function (endpoint) {
        if (JSON.parse(spApi.storageData('userLocation')).country !== 'undefined') {
            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{country}', JSON.parse(spApi.storageData('userLocation')).country);
            if (JSON.parse(spApi.storageData('userLocation')).city !== 'undefined') {
                endpoint = endpoint.replace('{city}', JSON.parse(spApi.storageData('userLocation')).city);
            }
        }

        return endpoint;
    };

    self.applyFeedTypesCondition = function (systemRulesFeedSources, xmlFeedSources) {
        return (!self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; xmlFeedSources.indexOf(self.feedSettings.feedSource) &gt; -1) ||
            (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; systemRulesFeedSources.indexOf(self.feedSettings.feedSource) &gt; -1);
    };

    self.generateEndpointItemId = function (endpoint, paidProducts) {
        if (['similarBought', 'checkoutRecommendation'].indexOf(self.feedSettings.feedSource) &gt; -1) {
            var itemIds = (paidProducts || []).map(function (product) {
                return product.id;
            }).join();

            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{itemId}', itemIds);

            if (self.feedSettings.feedSource === 'checkoutRecommendation') {
                var filterPrice = self.feedSettings.checkoutRecommendationCartValue - parseFloat(spApi.getTotalCartAmount());
                if (filterPrice &lt; 0) { // negative value
                    return false;
                }
                endpoint += '&amp;filter=[price.' + spApi.getCurrency() + '][&gt;=][' + filterPrice + ']';
            }
        } else {
            endpoint = endpoint.replace('{itemId}', (paidProducts[0] || {}).id);
        }

        return endpoint;
    };

    self.createCategoryInfo = function (endpoint, categories) {
        var newEndpoint = endpoint.replace('{category}', categories[0]);

        if (categories.length === 1) {
            newEndpoint = newEndpoint.replace('&amp;subcategory={subcategory}', '');
        } else if (categories.length &gt; 1) {
            newEndpoint = newEndpoint.replace('{subcategory}', categories[1]);
        }

        return newEndpoint;
    };

    self.getSalePrice = function (item) {
        var salePrice = '';

        if (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; item.original_price &amp;&amp; spApi.getCurrency()) {
            salePrice = isNaN(parseInt(item.original_price[spApi.getCurrency()])) ? item.original_price[spApi.getCurrency()] : item.price[spApi.getCurrency()];
        } else if (item.sale_price || item.item_price) {
            salePrice = isNaN(parseInt(item.sale_price)) ? item.item_price : item.sale_price;
        }

        return salePrice;
    };

    self.manageDynamicAttributes = function (item, itemContainer) {
        var itemProductAttr = item.product_attributes;

        if (camp.id === 0 || (typeof itemProductAttr !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; Object.keys(itemProductAttr).length &lt; 1)) {
            return false; // there is no attribute
        }

        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-attributes-container .ins-product-attribute-wrapper').each(function () {
            var dynamicElement = sQuery(this).find('.ins-dynamic-element-tag');
            var elementAttrName = sQuery(this).attr('data-element-name').replace('@', '');
            var attrValue = itemProductAttr[elementAttrName];

            if (attrValue) {
                var rgx = new RegExp('@' + elementAttrName, 'g');
                dynamicElement.html(sQuery(dynamicElement).html().replace(rgx, attrValue));
            } else {
                sQuery(this).css('display', 'none');
            }
        });
    };

    self.formatPrice = function (price) {
        var currencyRule = spApi.currencyFormatRules[spApi.getCurrency()];

        if (typeof currencyRule === 'undefined') {
            return price + ' ' + spApi.getCurrency();
        }

        price = price.toString();
        var floatingPrice = (price.split('.') || [])[1] || '';
        var basePrice = (price.split('.') || [])[0] || '';
        var formattedPrice = [];
        var percentile = 0;

        for (var i = (basePrice.length - 1); i &gt;= 0; i--) {
            if (percentile &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; percentile % 3 === 0) {
                formattedPrice.push(currencyRule.thousandSeparator);
                percentile = 0;
            }
            formattedPrice.push(basePrice[i]);
            percentile++;
        }
        basePrice = formattedPrice.reverse().join('');

        if (!floatingPrice) {
            return currencyRule.alignment === '1' ? basePrice + ' ' + currencyRule.symbol : currencyRule.symbol + ' ' + basePrice;
        }

        if (currencyRule.alignment === '1') {
            return basePrice + currencyRule.decimalSeparator + floatingPrice + ' ' + currencyRule.symbol;
        }

        return currencyRule.symbol + ' ' + basePrice + currencyRule.decimalSeparator + floatingPrice;
    };

    self.getSalePriceText = function (salePrice) {
        var formattedPrice = self.formatPrice(salePrice);

        return typeof salePrice === 'string' ? salePrice : formattedPrice;
    };

    self.getDiscountedPrice = function (item) {
        var priceAttr = self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule ? 'original_price' : 'item_price';

        if (!item[priceAttr]) {
            return '';
        }

        var priceType = priceAttr === "original_price" ? item[priceAttr][spApi.getCurrency()] : item[priceAttr];
        var formattedPrice = self.formatPrice(priceType);

        return typeof priceType === 'string' ? priceType : formattedPrice;
    };

    self.getOriginalPriceVisibility = function (item, salePrice) {
        if ('inline-block' === 'none') {
            return 'none';
        }

        if ((self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; !item.original_price) || (!self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule &amp;&amp; !item.item_price)) {
            return 'none';
        }

        var hideDiscount = self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule ? item.original_price[spApi.getCurrency()] === salePrice : item.item_price === salePrice;
        return hideDiscount ? 'none' : 'inline-block';

    };

    self.toCamelCase = function (text) {
        return text.toLowerCase().replace(/-(.)/g, function (match, word) {
            return word.toUpperCase();
        });
    };

    self.dynamicReplacement = function (productHtml, item, salePrice, addToCartButtonId) {
        var itemContainer = sQuery(productHtml);

        if (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule) {
            self.manageDynamicAttributes(item, itemContainer); // supports only system rule

            itemContainer.find('.ins-product-box').attr('href', camp.id !== 0 ? item.url : 'javascript:void(0);');
            itemContainer.find('.ins-image-box').css('background-image', 'url("' + item.image_url + '")');
            itemContainer.find('.ins-product-name').text(item.name);
            itemContainer.find('.ins-product-price').text(self.getSalePriceText(salePrice));
            itemContainer.find('.ins-product-discount').text(self.getDiscountedPrice(item));
            itemContainer.find('.ins-product-discount').css('display', self.getOriginalPriceVisibility(item, salePrice));
            itemContainer.find('.ins-add-to-cart-wrapper').attr('ins-product-id', item.item_id);
            itemContainer.html(itemContainer.html().replace('1508331698331', addToCartButtonId.toString()));

            return itemContainer[0].outerHTML;
        }

        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-box').attr('href', camp.id !== 0 ? item.item_url : 'javascript:void(0);');
        itemContainer.find('.ins-image-box').css('background-image', 'url("' + item.item_image + '")');
        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-name').text(item.item_name);
        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-price').text(self.getSalePriceText(salePrice));
        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-discount').text(self.getDiscountedPrice(item));
        itemContainer.find('.ins-product-discount').css('display', self.getOriginalPriceVisibility(item, salePrice));
        itemContainer.find('.ins-add-to-cart-wrapper').attr('ins-product-id', item.item_id);
        itemContainer.html(itemContainer.html().replace('1508331698331', addToCartButtonId.toString()));

        return itemContainer[0].outerHTML;
    };

    self.prepareProducts = function (data) {
        if (window.self !== window.top) {
            sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).hide();
        }

        var productHtml = sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-box-item:first').clone()[0].outerHTML;

        sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-box-item').remove();

        var addToCartButtonId = 1508331698331;

        sQuery(data).each(function (index, item) {
            if (index == self.feedSettings.feedSize) {
                return false;
            }

            sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-body').append(
                self.dynamicReplacement(productHtml, item, self.getSalePrice(item), addToCartButtonId)
            );

            //OPT-9380 start
            var productSelector = sQuery('.ins-preview-wrapper-665 .ins-product-box[href="' + item.url + '"]')
                .parents('.ins-selectable-element');

            if (item.product_attributes.ins_new_product) {
                productSelector.prepend('&lt;div class="ins-new-text"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            }

            if (item.product_attributes.ins_discounted_product) {
                productSelector.prepend('&lt;div class="ins-discount-text"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            }

            if (item.product_attributes.ins_product_star === 5) {
                productSelector.find('.ins-stars-img').attr('style', 'background: ' +
                    'url("https://image.useinsider.com/nyxcosmeticstr/c188/CjFoxdWtbNVZtsymiEe11548403212.png") ' +
                    'center center / contain no-repeat');
            }
            //OPT-9380 end

            addToCartButtonId++;
        });

    };

    self.getProductsFromPredictive = function (endpoint, callback) {
        if (endpoint) {
            sQuery.ajax({
                type: 'get',
                url: endpoint,
                success: function (response) {
                    if (self.insufficientProductCount(response)) {
                        sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).hide();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (self.isRecoFeedTypeSystemRule) {
                        callback(response.data);
                    } else {
                        callback(response);
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    };

    self.insufficientProductCount = function (response) {
        if (self.checkRecommendedProductSize(response) || self.checkIfProductNumberConsistency(response)) {
            return true; // no product
        }

        return false;
    };

    self.checkIfProductNumberConsistency = function (response) {
        var consistency = self.feedSettings.productConsistency;

        if (((typeof consistency === 'boolean' &amp;&amp; consistency) || consistency === 'true') &amp;&amp;
            ((typeof response.data !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; response.data.length &lt; self.feedSettings.feedSize) ||
                (typeof response !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; response.length &lt; self.feedSettings.feedSize))) {
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    };

    self.checkRecommendedProductSize = function (response) {
        if ((typeof response === 'undefined' &amp;&amp; response.length === 0) || (typeof response.data !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; response.data.length &lt; 1)) {
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    };

    self.sliderInit = function () {
        var smartRecommenderSlider = {};
        var touchStart, touchDefined;

        smartRecommenderSlider.elements = {
            wrapper: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-body-wrapper'),
            ul: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-body'),
            arrowWrapper: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-slider-arrow-wrapper'),
            next: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-slider-next .ins-slider-arrow-wrapper'),
            prev: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-slider-prev .ins-slider-arrow-wrapper'),
            contentWrapper: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).closest('.ins-content-wrapper'),
            productImageBox: sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-product-box .ins-image-box')
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.setDimensions = function () {
            var recommenderWrapperWidth = Number('') || this.elements.contentWrapper.width();

            this.elements.wrapper.width(recommenderWrapperWidth);
            this.elements.productImageBox.height('157' || '200px');

            this.windowItemCount = this.isResponsiveMode ? this.windowItemCount :
                (recommenderWrapperWidth / (this.eachItemWidth + this.betweenItemMargin));
            this.eachItemWidth = (recommenderWrapperWidth / this.windowItemCount) - this.betweenItemMargin;
            this.slidingItemCount = Number('1') || 1;
            this.isLoopActive = 'off' === 'true';

            this.elements.ul.find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-box-item').width(this.eachItemWidth);
            this.elements.ul.width((this.eachItemWidth + this.betweenItemMargin) * this.itemCount);

            this.elements.ul.attr('data-current', 0);

            return this;
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.construct = function () {
            this.betweenItemMargin = Number('5') * 2;
            this.eachItemWidth = Number('140') || 180;
            this.itemCount = sQuery(self.smartRecommenderMainWrapper).find('.ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-box-item').length;
            this.windowItemCount = Number('2');
            this.isResponsiveMode = 'false' === 'true';

            if (this.isResponsiveMode) {
                this.elements.wrapper.addClass('ins-responsive-mode-active');
            } else {
                this.elements.wrapper.removeClass('ins-responsive-mode-active');
            }

            this.setArrowIcons();
            this.setDimensions();
            this.bindEvents();
            this.bindTouchEvents();

            var rightToLeftLangList = [
                'ar_AE',
                'ar_AR',
                'ar_EG',
                'ar_ME',
                'ar_SA',
                'fa_FA',
                'ur_UR'
            ];

            if (!(rightToLeftLangList.indexOf(spApi.getLang()) &lt; 0)) {
                this.slideTo(this.itemCount - this.windowItemCount);
            }

            return this;
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.setArrowIcons = function () {
            var $arrowWrapper = this.elements.arrowWrapper;
            $arrowWrapper.removeClass('ins-arrow-with-background ins-arrow-with-border');

            if ('false' === 'true') {
                $arrowWrapper.addClass('ins-arrow-with-background');
            } else {
                $arrowWrapper.addClass('ins-arrow-with-border');
            }
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.checkArrowButtons = function () {
            var currentItem = this.elements.ul.attr('data-current');
            if (currentItem &lt; this.itemCount - this.windowItemCount) {
                this.elements.next.show();
            } else if (!this.isLoopActive) {
                this.elements.next.hide();
            }

            if (currentItem &gt; 0) {
                this.elements.prev.show();
            } else if (!this.isLoopActive) {
                this.elements.prev.hide();
            }
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.bindEvents = function () {
            this.checkArrowButtons();

            this.elements.prev.unbind();
            this.elements.next.unbind();

            this.elements.prev.click(this.slideToLeft.bind(this));

            this.elements.next.click(this.slideToRight.bind(this));
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.bindTouchEvents = function () {
            var element = this.elements.ul;
            var events = this.touchEvents;

            element.unbind('touchmove').on('touchmove', events.touchmove);

            element.unbind('touchstart').on('touchstart', events.touchstart);

            element.unbind('touchend').on('touchend', events.touchend);
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.touchEvents = {
            touchmove: function (event) {
                var xPos = event.originalEvent.touches[0].pageX;

                if (Math.abs(xPos - touchStart) &lt; 50) return;

                if (touchStart &gt; xPos &amp;&amp; typeof touchDefined === 'undefined') {
                    touchDefined = true;
                    smartRecommenderSlider.slideToRight();
                }
                if (touchStart &lt; xPos &amp;&amp; typeof touchDefined === 'undefined') {
                    touchDefined = true;
                    smartRecommenderSlider.slideToLeft();
                }
            },
            touchstart: function (event) {
                touchStart = event.originalEvent.touches[0].pageX;
            },
            touchend: function () {
                touchDefined = undefined;
                touchStart = undefined;
            }
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.slideTo = function (newCurrentItem) {
            this.elements.ul.attr('data-current', newCurrentItem);
            var newPosition = newCurrentItem * (this.eachItemWidth + this.betweenItemMargin);

            this.elements.ul.css({
                'transform': 'translateX(-' + newPosition + 'px)'
            });
            this.checkArrowButtons();
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.slideToLeft = function () {
            var currentItem = parseInt(this.elements.ul.attr('data-current'));
            var newCurrentItem = currentItem - this.slidingItemCount;

            if (newCurrentItem + this.slidingItemCount === 0) {
                if (!this.isLoopActive) {
                    return;
                }

                newCurrentItem = this.itemCount - Math.floor(this.windowItemCount);
            } else if (newCurrentItem &lt; 0) {
                newCurrentItem = 0;
            }

            this.slideTo(newCurrentItem);
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.slideToRight = function () {
            var currentItem = parseInt(this.elements.ul.attr('data-current'));
            var newCurrentItem = currentItem + this.slidingItemCount;
            var windowItemCount = Math.floor(this.windowItemCount);
            var itemCount = Math.floor(this.itemCount);
            var emptyAreaCount = Math.abs(windowItemCount - this.slidingItemCount);

            if (newCurrentItem + emptyAreaCount &gt;= itemCount) {
                if (!this.isLoopActive) {
                    return;
                }

                newCurrentItem = 0;
            } else if (itemCount - newCurrentItem &lt; windowItemCount) {
                newCurrentItem = itemCount - windowItemCount;
            }

            this.slideTo(newCurrentItem);
        };

        smartRecommenderSlider.construct();

        return smartRecommenderSlider;
    };

    self.setEvents = function (recommenderSlider) {
        // Add To Cart Event
        if (camp.id !== 0) {
            sQuery('.ins-add-to-cart-wrapper').unbind('click.insRecoAddToCart').on('click.insRecoAddToCart', function () {
                spApi.spAddToCart().addToBasket(sQuery(this).attr('ins-product-id'));
            });
        } else {
            // After appending new data element list has to update
            setTimeout(function () {
                ActionBuilder.eventManager.triggerManualEvent('notification.refreshElementList');
            }, 200);
        }

        sQuery(window).off('resize.' + camp.id)
            .on('resize.' + camp.id, spApi.debounce(recommenderSlider.setDimensions.bind(recommenderSlider), 100));
    };

    self.construct = function () {
        var endpoint = self.getProductFeedEndpoint();

        if (endpoint === false) {
            return false;
        }

        self.getProductsFromPredictive(endpoint, function (data) {
            self.prepareProducts(data);

            sQuery('.ins-preview-wrapper-' + camp.id + ' .ins-mobile-web-smart-recommender-main-wrapper').show();

            var slider = self.sliderInit();

            self.setEvents(slider);
        });
    };

    self.construct();

    sQuery(document).on('framelessInited' + camp.id, function () {
        self.construct();
    });
})({});
